  OFFICE OF ADMINISTRATOR REHABILITATION &  RESETTLEMENT SCHEME AND  REVENUE DIVISIONAL                    
                                                                OFFICER, ILLUPPUR DIVISION, PUDUKKOTTAI DISTRICT. 
 
 
 Cauvery – Vaigai – Gundar Canal Link Scheme, Pudukottai District.
REHABILITATION AND RESETTLEMENT SCHEME
(Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 2013 Section 16(2) and 
Tamil Nadu Land Acquisitions Rules 2017 Rule 15(2)
(R.C. No. A3/623/2020)
(ந.க. 351/அ2/ைவ.þ./2022)
 An extent of 17.34.35 Hec. of wet, Dry and Manavari lands in Mathur Village of Kulathur Taluk in Pudukkottai District is 
needed or is likely to be needed for a public purpose namely formation of Cauvery – Vaigai – Gundar Canal Link scheme in 
accordance with the Primary Notiﬁ cation issued u/s 11(1) of RFCTLARR Act 2013 published in the Pudukottai District Gazette 
No. 1, date 03.01.2022 (Collector, Pudukkottai Roc.164/2021(CVG)/A2 dated.31.12.2021). As per Section 16(2) of RFCTLARR 
Act and 15(2) of Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Rules, 2017 and as per the survey and census conducted, a Rehabilitation 
and Resettlement Plan is prepared as under having three parts namely basic details for the scheme, Entitlements under 
Resettlement and Rehabilitation Schedule and Provision of Infrastructure Amenities

Cauvery–Vaigai–Gundar Canal Link Scheme, Pudukottai District.
REHABILITATION AND RESETTLEMENT SCHEME
(Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 2013 section 16(2) 
and Tamil Nadu Land Acquisitions Rules 2017 Rule 15(2)):
An extent of 33.28.73  Hec.  of Wet, Dry and Manavari lands in Poongudi Village of Kulathur  Taluk in Pudukkottai 
District is needed or is likely to be needed for a public purpose namely formation of  Cauver–Vaigai–Gundar Canal 
Link Scheme in accordance with the Primary Notiﬁ cation issued u/s 11(1) of RFCTLARR Act 2013 published in the 
Pudukottai District Gazette No. 6 date 04.03.2022 (District Collector Pudukkottai  Roc.A2/121/2022 C/V/G/ 2022 Dated.25.02.2022). 
As per Section 16(2) of RFCTLARR Act and 15(2) of Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Rules 2017 and as per the survey and 
census conducted, a Rehabilitation and Resettlement Plan is prepared as under having three parts namely basic details for 
the scheme, Entitlements under Resettlement and Rehabilitation Schedule and Provision of Infrastructure Amenities.

Public Hearing:
A public hearing meeting is scheduled to be conducted by the Administrator, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Scheme 
and Revenue Divisional Oﬃ  cer, Illuppur at Devibala Thirumanamandabam, Taluk oﬃ  ce Road, Keeranur on 14.10.2022 
at 10.30 A.M.  The land owners whose lands are to be acquired shall raise their objections/ requests if any, regarding 
the Rehabilitation and Resettlement Scheme.

The entitlements under Rehabilitation and Resettlement Scheme are to be disbursed to the aﬀ ected families within 6

Cauvery–Vaigai–Gundar Canal Link scheme, Pudukottai District.
REHABILITATION  AND  RESETTLEMENT  SCHEME
(Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 2013 section 16(2) 
and Tamil Nadu Land Acquisitions Rules 2017 Rule 15(2))
An extent of  17.28.05 Hec.  of wet, Dry and Manavari lands in Vazhamangalam Village of Kulathur Taluk in 
Pudukkottai District is needed or is likely to be needed for a public purpose namely formation of  Cauvery–Vaigai–Gundar 
Canal Link Scheme in accordance with the Primary Notiﬁ cation issued u/s 11(1) of RFCTLARR Act 2013 published in the 
Pudukottai District Gazette No. 15 date 13.05.2022(Collector Pudukkottai Roc. 222/A2/C.V.G/2022 Dated.29.04.2022). 
As per Section 16(2) of RFCTLARR Act and 15(2) of Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Rules 2017 and asper the survey and 
census conducted, a Rehabilitation and Resettlement Plan is prepared as under having three parts namely basic details for 
the scheme, Entitlements under Resettlement and Rehabilitation Schedule and Provision of Infrastructure Amenities
